name:sâ€hâ€aâ€wâ€x
info:Deluxe Executive Room (Double bed)
info:Stayed in November 2023
info:Couples
info:76 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted November 12, 2023
msg:An unexpected surprise, a very good hotel. I used to stay at Jinling when I came to Pizhou because I trusted its brand. This time I wanted to try something new, but I didn't expect to find a rare good hotel. First of all, the room type is good. The executive deluxe room is not much more expensive, but the bed is super big. It is not an exaggeration to sleep four people. Sleeping alone will make you feel lonely. The decoration style is also good. Secondly, the service is good. Similar to the resort hotel in Sanya, there is a one-to-one contact service before check-in. Yogurt and fruit are prepared in the guest room before check-in. Slippers and mineral water are also placed at the head of the bed. The breakfast buffet has not been selected yet, and the hot towel has been placed on the seat. After the meal, when I returned to the room, the room had been cleaned. While serving with all my heart, I did not let the customers feel disturbed. To be honest, the service has completely surpassed the standards of Marriott, IHG and other chain luxury hotels, and even surpassed the standards of resort hotels in tourist resorts. I have stayed in countless high, medium and low-end hotels at home and abroad, and I have never found such a caring hotel, nor have I ever felt so surprised. At the same time, Platinum Cui has a high cost-effectiveness. Although the price is not cheap in a small county, it is worth it with such hardware and services. It even made me give up the idea of â€‹â€‹staying in a chain brand in Xuzhou city. Finally, if I have to nitpick, there are two shortcomings. First, there is only one exit of the parking lot, the guardrail is narrow and it is easy to pass by cars, which is not very convenient. It is recommended to transform another channel into an automatic identification unattended one, which can also be used by guests staying in the hotel, or expand the existing exit; second, after check-in, two staff members take turns to provide contact services. They are enthusiastic, but a little disturbing. After training, they can uniformly reduce the frequency of contact with customers. It is enough to contact customers once in advance for relevant matters. Fruit yogurt can be put directly into the guest room after cleaning, without repeated confirmation. The above is generally a very, very good hotel, and it is a must-choose when you come to Pizhou in the future.
